                      <p>
                       CCI postdoctoral researcher Douglas Lee was selected to present at Drexel's annual International Research Showcase in Behrakis Grand Hall on May 26. Lee presented his poster titled "Simulating Human Performance with Delegation Assignment and Coordination" (co-authored by CCI computer science student Daniel Fitzick and Professor Ellen Bass).
